<analysis>**original_problem_statement:**
The user initially requested to fix a list of 7 bugs related to UI/UX, navigation, and backend errors. After the bugs were fixed, the user provided new, detailed requirements for two major features:
1.  **Email Management:** Enhance privacy by showing only relevant emails to the logged-in user and allow manual association of emails to a client file.
2.  **AI Document Data Validation:** Implement a system to handle data conflicts when the AI extracts information from a document that clashes with existing data. This includes getting user confirmation to accept or reject the AI's suggestions and a flag to lock a client's data from further AI modifications.

**what currently exists?**
The application is a process management CRM. In this session, the agent successfully fixed a batch of 7 critical bugs and implemented two major features requested by the user.

7.  **UI:** Resolved general formatting issues on the process details screen.

**New Features Implemented:**
1.  **AI Data Conflict Resolution:** A system is now in place to detect and manage conflicts between data extracted by AI and existing client data. A new UI component allows users to review these conflicts and choose which data to keep.
2.  **Enhanced Email Management:** The email history panel now only shows emails relevant to the logged-in user, and a new feature allows for the manual association of emails with a client file.

All fixes and features were validated by the testing agent and passed all tests.
